### [287] [BioRefusalAudit: Auditing Biosecurity Refusal Depth Using General and Domain-Fine-Tuned Sparse Autoencoders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30162)
*Caleb DeLeeuw*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究发现大模型的生物安全拒绝机制极易受提示词格式与长度影响而失效，且普遍存在过度拒绝合法内容的现象。研究提出利用稀疏自编码器（SAE）进行内部特征审计，能有效揭示行为评估无法发现的模型安全失败模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前生物安全评估多关注模型是否产生有害输出，而忽略了模型“拒绝”行为本身的结构稳健性。作者旨在探究模型在面对提示词格式微调、长度限制或不同文化敏感性内容时，其拒绝机制是否会失效或产生过度拒绝。

Method: 研究通过对比五个不同架构的模型（Gemma 2, Gemma 4, Qwen 2.5, Phi-3, Llama 3.2）在多种提示词格式、长度约束及不同危害级别（包括合法的生物学知识）下的表现，评估拒绝机制的稳健性。此外，引入“发散分数”（Divergence score）概念，利用稀疏自编码器（SAE）监测模型内部特征激活，以区分表面的拒绝行为与其内部的潜在逻辑。

Result: 结果显示没有模型能完美区分良性与有害请求。Gemma模型对格式极为敏感（如移除模板后拒绝率归零），且在长度限制下拒绝机制完全崩溃；Qwen与Phi-3表现出明显的过度拒绝现象；部分模型对合法生物学研究的拒绝率甚至高于有害内容，反映其拒绝逻辑倾向于遵循合法性与文化显著性而非实质危害。SAE分析表明，内部激活特征可以有效区分合规与拒绝行为，即便在行为层面难以分辨。

Conclusion: 现有的语言模型安全拒绝机制在面对微小的提示词框架、格式或长度调整时表现极其不稳定。基于激活值的审计（如使用稀疏自编码器SAE）能揭示模型行为层面上不可见的拒绝逻辑缺陷，是评估大模型生物安全性的重要补充手段。

Abstract: Biosecurity evaluations of language models typically ask whether models produce hazardous output. This paper asks a complementary question: when a model refuses, is that refusal structurally sound, or does it disappear under modest changes to prompt framing, formatting, or output length? Across five architectures, no model cleanly discriminated benign from hazard. Gemma 2 2B-IT never genuinely refused across 75 prompts, hedging on every hazard-adjacent query. Gemma 4 E2B-IT refused 65/75 prompts with chat-template formatting and 0/75 without it. Both Gemma models collapsed to 0% under an 80-token cap. Qwen 2.5 1.5B and Phi-3-mini over-refused, flagging 83-87% of benign biology as hazardous. Llama 3.2 1B showed the only meaningful tier gradient (61-point spread). To probe what drives such over-refusal, we tested a panel of Schedule I but biologically non-toxic compounds (notably psilocybin cultivation, with FDA Breakthrough Therapy status). Some models refused these at rates exceeding genuinely hazardous biology, suggesting refusal tracks legality and cultural salience over CBRN hazard. To measure the internal side, we introduce a divergence score D comparing a model's surface response label to its internal sparse autoencoder (SAE) feature activations. Full D was computed on Gemma 2 2B-IT (Gemma Scope 1) and Gemma 4 E2B-IT (author-trained bio SAE). Two fine-tuned Gemma 2 domain SAEs were released. On Gemma 4, comply and refuse responses separated by a 0.647-point gap with zero overlap (n=75), though this is preliminary, with a narrow catalog, within-sample calibration, and Gemma-family-only SAE coverage. Built over one hackathon weekend on consumer hardware (GTX 1650 Ti Max-Q, plus Colab T4 for SAE training), this preliminary evidence suggests activation-level auditing may surface failure modes invisible to behavioral evaluation, with substantial variation across architectures.

### [288] [Double-Edged Sword or Sharp Tool? Designing and Evaluating Triadic LLM-Teacher Collaboration for K-12 Writing at Scale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30200)
*Canran Wang,Yuwen Yang,Zhen Wang,Ming Ma,Ding Yu,Chentai Wang,Keman Huang,Xiaoyong Du*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究通过大规模实证分析，构建了“LLM-教师-学生”三元协作机制，证实了AI辅助写作教学的有效性，并强调了根据学生水平动态调整协作策略以避免过度依赖（上限效应）的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究开发了一个支持K-12写作学习的三元协作系统，并基于系统功能语言学（SFL）构建了多维评估框架及建议轨迹追踪流水线。通过对跨度两年、涉及120所学校、10,195名学生的57,954篇作文进行大规模实证分析，验证了该协作模式的有效性。

Result: 实验结果表明，该协作系统显著提升了学生的写作质量。研究明确了LLM作为生成引擎能有效降低教师工作负荷，而教师作为教学把关人和沟通桥梁对保证反馈质量至关重要。研究还揭示了“语言扩展上限效应”，即过度使用LLM进行润色并不能无限制提升写作能力。

Conclusion: 本研究通过构建“LLM-教师-学生”三元协作机制，证实了在K-12写作教学中，通过合理的角色分工（LLM辅助生成、教师把关指导），能够有效提升学生的写作质量。同时指出，随着学生水平的提升，过度依赖LLM的语言扩展会产生边际效用递减的“上限效应”，因此协作模式应随学生的成长动态调整。

Abstract: The double-edged sword of integrating Large Language Models (LLMs) requires an effective triadic collaboration mechanism among LLMs, teachers and students, especially for K-12 education. By developing a triadic collaboration system to support K-12 writing learning, a multidimensional evaluation framework grounded in Systemic Functional Linguistics and the suggestion trajectory tracing pipeline, this paper contributes a large-scale empirical dataset involving $57,954$ essays from $10,195$ students across $120$ schools over two years. Our findings confirm the efficacy of this system in improving writing quality through a strategic labor division: the LLM serves as a generative engine to mitigate teacher burnout, and the teacher acts as a pedagogical gatekeeper and bridge to guarantee feedback quality. While both LLM and teacher are critical for skill improvement, we uncover a ceiling effect where excessive linguistic expansion yields diminishing marginal utility. These suggest a dynamically adaptive LLM-teacher collaboration as student proficiency increases.

### [289] [When Should Models Change Their Minds? Contextual Belief Management in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30219)
*Haoming Xu,Weihong Xu,Zongrui Li,Mengru Wang,Yunzhi Yao,Chiyu Wu,Jin Shang,Yu Gong,Shumin Deng*

Motivation: 现有的语言模型在处理长周期交互时，往往难以处理不断积累的信息，难以精准判断何时更新状态、何时维持现有状态以及如何忽略不相关的噪声，导致性能下降。作者旨在定量化这种“情境置信管理”能力并寻找提升方案。

Method: 1. 提出了“情境置信管理（CBM）”概念，用于建模长周期任务中的状态维护问题。
2. 构建了“BeliefTrack”基准测试，涵盖规则发现和电路诊断任务，利用符号验证器进行Turn-level的精确评估。
3. 诊断了模型的三种典型失效：未更新（Failed Update）、误更新（Failed Stay）和未能忽略噪声（Failed Isolation）。
4. 实验对比了基准模型、提示工程（Prompting）、基于置信奖励的强化学习（RL）以及表征层干预（Steering）的效果。

Result: 1. 传统LLM在CBM任务上表现较差，且简单的提示工程提升有限。
2. 引入基于置信状态奖励的强化学习，平均故障率降低了70.9%。
3. 通过表征层干预（Representation-level steering），在两项任务中的故障率平均降低了46.1%。

Conclusion: LLM在处理长周期交互任务时，目前普遍缺乏对状态的有效管理能力。通过引入显式的置信状态监督（如强化学习奖励或表征控制），可以显著提升模型在保持、更新及过滤信息方面的准确性，从而实现更鲁棒的长期任务规划。

Abstract: Long-horizon interactions require language models to manage accumulating information: when to update their state, when to preserve their state, and what to ignore. We study this challenge as \textbf{Contextual Belief Management (CBM)}: maintaining a predicted belief state aligned with formal evidence while isolating task-irrelevant noise. To make CBM measurable, we introduce BeliefTrack, a closed-world benchmark spanning Rule Discovery and Circuit Diagnosis, where a finite belief space and symbolic verifiers enable exact turn-level evaluation. BeliefTrack diagnoses three failures: Failed Stay, Failed Update, and Failed Isolation. Across multiple LLMs, vanilla models exhibit severe CBM failures, while explicit belief-tracking prompts provide limited gains. In contrast, reinforcement learning with belief-state rewards reduces failure rates by 70.9\% on average. Further probing reveals latent belief-state dynamics behind these failures, and representation-level steering reduces failure rates by 46.1\% across two tasks\footnote{Code is coming soon at https://github.com/zjunlp/CBM.

</details>

*Peter W. Rose,Benjamin M. Good,Amanda M. Saravia-Butler,Charlotte A. Nelson,James P. Balhoff,Yaphet Kebede,Patricia L. Whetzel,Christopher Bizon,Andrew I. Su,Sergio E. Baranzini*

Result: 成功构建了一个开源的 MCP 服务器，使用户能够通过自然语言高效地查询、集成和分析多个科学知识图谱，并提供了完整的文档、配置指南及示例以支持社区使用。

Conclusion: mcp-proto-okn 为人工智能助手提供了一种标准化的科学知识图谱交互接口，成功简化了跨领域知识图谱的分析流程，促进了科学数据与AI应用之间的互操作性。

Abstract: MCP Server Proto-OKN (mcp-proto-okn) is a Python-based Model Context Protocol server that enables AI assistants to discover, inspect, query and integrate scientific knowledge graphs through natural language. The server provides graph routing, schema inspection, SPARQL execution, ontology expansion, multi-graph querying, and transcript generation, lowering the barrier to cross-domain knowledge graph analysis for biomedical and scientific users.
  mcp-proto-okn is implemented in Python using the FastMCP framework and is available at https://github.com/sbl-sdsc/mcp-proto-okn. Documentation, client configuration instructions, and example analysis transcripts are provided in the GitHub repository.

### [291] [The Cognitive Categorical Transformer: Category-Theoretic Inductive Biases for Language Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28864)
*Al Kari*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 研究提出CCT架构，通过将范畴论中的“单纯复形消息传递”整合进GPT-2，在WikiText-103上显著提升了困惑度，并揭示了唯有改变拓扑结构的先验才有助于改善语言模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在通过引入范畴论与认知科学的理论组件，突破传统Transformer架构在处理语言建模时的局限，并探讨哪些类型的范畴先验能够真正提升模型性能，解决模型架构设计中结构信息表达不足的问题。

Method: 作者提出了认知范畴Transformer（CCT）架构，在预训练的GPT-2 Small骨干模型基础上，集成了基于范畴论和认知科学的组件。核心方法包括引入GT-Full单纯复形消息传递机制，并对比了包括层级平滑、伴随往返和曲率正则化在内的多种范畴先验。通过在WikiText-103数据集上进行匹配步长的训练与消融实验进行验证。

Result: CCT模型（306M参数）在WikiText-103验证集上达到了21.27的困惑度（PPL），相比相同配置的GPT-2 Small基准（24.19 PPL）提升了12%（降低了2.92 PPL）。消融实验显示，84%的性能提升归功于GT-Full单纯复形消息传递机制。

Conclusion: 该研究确立了“结构/一致性区分”原则：引入新拓扑结构的范畴论先验（如GT-Full）能有效提升语言模型性能，而仅强制执行一致性恒等式的先验则效果不佳。此外，该研究首次在306M参数规模下证实了单纯复形消息传递（Simplicial Message Passing）对困惑度的改善作用。

Abstract: The Cognitive Categorical Transformer (CCT) is a 306M-parameter architecture that augments a pretrained GPT-2 Small backbone with cognitively grounded components derived from category theory and several inspirations from cognitive science. Under a matched-step protocol (215,000 optimizer steps, matched data, matched optimizer and schedule) on WikiText-103, CCT reaches 21.27 validation perplexity, compared with 24.19 for an identically fine-tuned GPT-2 Small baseline. The architecture therefore contributes a 2.92 PPL (12% relative) reduction beyond what in-domain fine-tuning alone provides. A retrain-from-scratch ablation that holds GT-Full simplicial message passing bypassed across the entire seven-phase activation schedule reaches 23.72 PPL, localizing 84% of the architectural improvement (2.45 of 2.92 PPL) to GT-Full. We present the first ablation-validated evidence that simplicial message passing improves language-model perplexity at the 306M-parameter scale on WikiText-103. Published GPT-2 Large reaches 22.05 zero-shot PPL on WikiText-103 with 6.2x more parameters than GPT-2 Small; this paper treats that number as an external published reference, not as the architectural benchmark. Three negative results on consistency-style categorical priors (sheaf smoothing, adjunction round-trip, curvature regularization) and the joint structural-prior result for GT-Full and PrecisionWeightedPP together support an empirical pattern termed the *structure/consistency distinction*, in which categorical priors that add new topology improve language modeling and those that enforce a consistency identity do not.

</details>


### [292] [ProjectionBench: Evaluating Scientific Hypothesis Generation in LLMs Under Progressive Information Disclosure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30284)
*A. J. Lew,Y. Cao,M. J. Buehler*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个针对科学发现任务的LLM评估基准，通过“逐步披露实验细节”的方式测试模型的创新推理能力，并对当前顶尖模型在材料科学领域的表现进行了实证分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基准测试多侧重于多跳检索，无法充分评估大语言模型（LLM）在科学发现中所需的创造性推理和超越已知知识的科研能力。因此，需要建立一个能够衡量模型在科学研究全过程中表现的新框架。

Method: 提出了一种分阶段的信息披露评估框架。模型首先仅获得研究主题和问题，随后逐步披露实验细节。在每个阶段，要求模型生成假设，并通过自动化语义相似度分析将其与原始论文结论进行对比。该方法通过评估语义偏离度，衡量了模型从“极简信息下的创新性”到“完全实验细节下的基础推理能力”。

Result: 通过对生物活性材料、机械材料和纳米材料领域的45篇论文进行评估，发现GPT-5.4和Gemini 3.1 pro的表现优于前代模型。特别是GPT-5.4，在仅有极简上下文的情况下，依然能保持与真实科研结论0.7的F1对齐分数。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一个能够系统评估大语言模型在科学发现中创新推理能力的新基准框架。实验表明，更先进的模型（如GPT-5.4和Gemini 3.1 pro）在处理科学问题时表现更优，尤其是在信息有限的情况下，模型仍能保持一定程度的逻辑对齐。该框架为评估AI科学家的研究能力提供了重要的衡量工具。

Abstract: Scientific discovery is an inherently creative and uncertain process, requiring reasoning beyond the recall of known knowledge. While many benchmarks have been proposed to evaluate large language model (LLM) performance on deep research tasks via multi-hop retrieval, their innovative reasoning abilities essential for true scientific discovery remain largely untested. We introduce a benchmark framework for evaluating model performance in scientific discovery and reasoning, building up from a raw problem to the classical null hypothesis test. In our framework, models initially receive only the topic and research question from a recent paper, with technical details progressively revealed. At each stage of information disclosure, the model is tasked with generating hypotheses that address the research question, which is compared with the conclusions from the original paper and evaluated via automated semantic similarity of constituent atomic claims. This progressive evaluation of semantic divergence from ground-truth conclusions enables assessment of a model's innovativeness (under minimal information) to grounded reasoning capabilities (under full experimental details), both critical for using LLMs for scientific discovery purposes. Our framework provides a foundation for systematically evaluating scientific reasoning and discovery capabilities in LLMs, crucial for advancing the development of next-generation AI scientist/co-scientist systems. Specifically, here we evaluate GPT-5, GPT-5.4, Gemini 2.5 pro, and Gemini 3.1 pro preview across 45 papers spanning bioactive materials, mechanical materials, and nanomaterials. We find that GPT-5.4 and Gemini 3.1 pro outperform their previous generation counterparts as expected, and GPT-5.4 in particular maintains 0.7 F1 score alignment with ground truth conclusions even under minimal context.

### [293] [MIRA: Mid-training Rubric Anchoring for Source-Aware Data Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30288)
*Haowen Wang,Yaxin Du,Jian Yang,Jiajun Wu,Shukai Liu,Yuxuan Zhang,Pingjie Wang,Siheng Chen,Tuney Zheng,Ming Zhou,Xianglong Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对大模型中期训练的数据筛选难题，本文提出了MIRA框架。通过自动发现不同数据源的评估准则并将其转化为可扩展的评分模型，MIRA显著提升了筛选效率和模型性能，在代码任务中以50%的数据量达到了全量训练的效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大模型的中期训练（mid-training）阶段，现有的数据选择方法存在两难：基于模型的方法（如损失预测）虽然具备可扩展性但缺乏明确的语义判断，而语义筛选方法虽然判断力强但受限于固定的准则或标准化格式。作者旨在解决这一矛盾，以提升大规模异构数据筛选的质量和针对性。

Method: 提出了一种名为MIRA的源感知筛选框架，核心在于“自锚定准则发现”（self-anchored rubric discovery）。该方法首先通过模型针对不同的数据源组自动发现评估准则，随后将这些判断蒸馏为可扩展的学生评分模型，从而对整个语料库进行高效筛选。

Result: 在代码领域的中期训练实验中，MIRA在21个数据源和5个源组上进行测试，在9个代码基准测试中超越了现有的数据选择基准方法；此外，MIRA仅使用了一半的训练令牌（tokens）就达到了使用全量数据进行训练的性能水平。

Conclusion: MIRA通过将评估准则发现与数据筛选过程相结合，有效解决了大规模预训练数据筛选中缺乏源自适应性和评价标准的问题，证明了通过自我锚定评估机制可以实现高效、高质量的数据筛选，为LLM的中期训练提供了一种更具可扩展性和针对性的方案。

Abstract: Mid-training has become an important stage in modern LLM development, using large-scale curated mixtures to strengthen capabilities before final post-training. Its data selection problem is distinct: the data are optimized under a pretraining-style objective at near-pretraining scale, but are curated toward downstream capabilities and drawn from heterogeneous sources with different formats and training roles. As a result, effective selection requires both scalability and source-adaptive semantic criteria. Existing model-based methods scale well, but provide only implicit quality signals. Semantic selection methods offer stronger judgments, but usually assume fixed rubrics or standardized data formats. To address this mismatch, we propose MIRA, a source-aware filtering framework based on self-anchored rubric discovery. The key idea is to make rubric construction part of data selection: MIRA first discovers what should be evaluated for each source group, then distills those judgments into scalable student scorers for full-corpus filtering. On code-oriented mid-training with 21 sources and 5 source groups, MIRA outperforms selection baselines across nine code benchmarks and matches the full-corpus run while using only half the tokens.

</details>


### [294] [Demystifying Data Organization for Enhanced LLM Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30334)
*Yalun Dai,Yangyu Huang,Tongshen Yang,Yonghan Wang,Xin Zhang,Wenshan Wu,Qihao Zhao,Hao Li,Yuanyuan Gao,Kim-Hui Yap,Scarlett Li*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然数据筛选已得到广泛研究，但数据组织（如何编排数据流）在大型语言模型训练中仍未被充分利用，且当前训练通常仅限于少量 epoch，因此亟需探索如何通过高效的数据组织提升训练效果。

Method: 研究提出了四项数据组织准则：边界锐化、循环调度、课程连续性及局部多样性；并基于此设计了两种新型数据排序方法（STR 和 SAW），通过重用预计算的样本级评分来实现数据流的有效组织。

Result: 在不同模型规模和数据规模下（涵盖预训练和指令微调阶段）的广泛实验证明，所提出的数据组织准则和方法有效提升了模型的收敛速度、训练稳定性和最终性能。

Conclusion: 研究表明，数据组织策略（即训练数据的排列顺序）对大型语言模型的训练效率和最终性能具有显著影响。通过遵循提出的四项组织准则（边界锐化、循环调度、课程连续性、局部多样性），可以无需额外大规模算力开销，显著提升模型训练的稳定性和性能。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have revolutionized various fields, yet their training efficiency is heavily reliant on effective data curation. While data selection has been widely studied, the strategic data organization for enhanced training remains an underexplored area, particularly since current LLMs are often trained for only one or a few epochs. This paper systematically explores the influence of data organization on LLM training by reusing pre-computed sample-level scores originally generated for data efficiency, thereby incurring minimal additional computational overhead. We identify and formalize four key guidelines for optimizing data organization: Boundary Sharpening, Cyclic Scheduling, Curriculum Continuity, and Local Diversity. Guided by them, we introduce two novel data ordering methods termed STR and SAW. Extensive experiments across different model scales and data sizes, encompassing both pre-training and SFT stages, validate the effectiveness of our summarized guidelines. They also demonstrate the robustness of our proposed data ordering methods in enhancing the stability and performance of LLM training. Github Link: https://github.com/microsoft/data-efficacy/

### [295] [Robust and Efficient Guardrails with Latent Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29068)
*Siddharth Sai,Xiaofei Wen,Muhao Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: COLAGUARD通过将复杂的多步安全推理过程压缩进连续的潜空间，实现了高效的安全护栏，在保持高准确率的同时，大幅降低了推理延迟和计算成本，解决了大模型安全防御在实际高吞吐应用中的性能瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的LLM安全护栏方案中，基于分类的方法效果有限，而基于推理（reasoning-based）的方法虽然效果好，但存在高查询延迟和高Token消耗的问题，难以在实际的高吞吐场景中应用。因此，需要一种既能保持高性能推理能力，又能实现高效部署的护栏方案。

Method: 本文提出了COLAGUARD护栏模型。其核心方法是通过阶段性训练课程（stage-wise training curriculum），将多步安全推理过程转化为连续的潜空间（continuous latent space）表示，从而在推理阶段实现直接的隐藏状态传播（hidden-state propagation），避免了显式生成推理文本带来的高延迟和高开销。

Result: 在八个安全基准测试的十个提示/回复审核设置中，COLAGUARD的Macro-F1指标比Llama Guard 3提高了8.24个点，并达到了与显式推理基线GuardReasoner相当的效果；同时，推理速度提升了12.9倍，Token消耗减少了22.4倍。

Conclusion: 研究表明，潜空间推理（latent reasoning）为可部署的安全护栏提供了一种实用的替代方案。通过将推理过程转化为潜空间表示，可以在不牺牲安全性的前提下，显著提升推理效率，证明了安全鲁棒性和推理效率可以实现同步优化，而非此消彼长。

Abstract: Maintaining the safety of large language models (LLMs) is crucial as they are increasingly deployed in real-world applications. Existing safety guardrails typically rely on single-pass classification or, more recently, distilled reasoning. Reasoning-based guardrails significantly outperform classification-only baselines, but they incur substantial query latency and token overhead that make them impractical for highthroughput deployment. To address this challenge, we propose COLAGUARD, a guardrail model that transfers multi-step safety reasoning into a continuous latent space through a stage-wise training curriculum, enabling direct hidden-state propagation at inference. Evaluated on ten prompt- and response-moderation settings spanning eight safety benchmarks, COLAGUARD improves macro-F1 by 8.24 points over Llama Guard 3 and matches our explicit reasoning baseline, GuardReasoner, in macroF1 while delivering a 12.9X speedup and 22.4X reduction in token usage. Our results suggest that latent reasoning offers a practical alternative to explicit rationale generation for deployable guardrails, jointly improving safety robustness and inference efficiency rather than treating them as competing objectives.

To address this gap, we construct VisAnomBench, a curated benchmark built from public time-series datasets and augmented with high-quality anomaly explanations selected from multiple large VLMs using fine-grained, task-specific rewards. Through fine-tuning on this benchmark, we develop VisAnomReasoner, a parameter-efficient VLM for time-series anomaly detection. Experimental results on VisAnomBench show that VisAnomReasoner achieves more accurate anomaly localization and consistently outperforms all baselines, with improvements of at least 21.23 and 23.87 percentage points in precision and F1, respectively. ### [297] [SchGen: PCB Schematic Generation with Semantic-Grounded Code Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30345)
*Qinpei Luo,Ruichun Ma,Xinyu Zhang,Lili Qiu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为SchGen的专用大语言模型，通过引入全新的语义化原理图表征方法，成功实现了从自然语言指令到可编辑PCB原理图的自动化生成，解决了传统硬件设计格式难以被模型理解的难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: PCB原理图设计高度依赖人工且门槛高，目前缺乏针对PCB原理图的生成式AI工具。现有的原理图格式（如工具特定的网表或几何格式）过于冗长且难以直接被大模型处理，因此需要一种新型表征方法和大规模数据集来推动该领域的发展。

Method: 1. 提出一种语义化的代码表征：将原理图的几何描述转换为基于编辑原语、相对位置和引脚命名连接的语义表示，降低了生成难度；2. 构建大规模数据集：通过人机协作流水线，将开源硬件设计转化为该语义表示并与自然语言提示配对；3. 训练专用大模型SchGen：利用该表示法进行针对性训练，优化模型在原理图生成任务上的表现。

Result: 实验结果显示，SchGen模型在原理图布线准确性和功能正确性方面显著优于现有的其他表征方法以及通用的基础大语言模型，证明了该方法在解决硬件设计生成任务上的有效性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，通过设计专门的语义化表征，能够有效克服传统EDA格式的复杂性，使大语言模型在处理复杂的硬件设计任务（如PCB原理图生成）时表现出极高的准确性和功能正确性，证明了表征学习对专用领域生成式模型的重要性。

Abstract: Printed circuit board (PCB) schematic design defines nearly all electronic hardware, but it remains manual and expertise-intensive. While generative AI has advanced digital and analog IC design, PCB schematic generation from natural-language intent is largely unexplored. This paper presents SchGen, the first large language model that generates editable PCB schematics from natural-language requests. The key challenge lies in the lack of an LLM-suited representation and a large-scale dataset. Current schematic formats are dominated by verbose, tool-specific syntax and geometry-heavy descriptions, making them difficult to generate reliably. We introduce a semantically grounded code representation that encodes schematic editing primitives with relative placement and pin-name-based wiring, transforming a geometry-driven generation problem into a semantics-driven matching task amenable to LLMs. We further construct a large-scale dataset of PCB schematics paired with user prompts via a human-agent collaborative pipeline that converts open-source hardware designs into our representation. Experiments show that SchGen significantly outperforms alternative representations and even larger general-purpose LLMs on wire connectivity accuracy and functional correctness. Our results highlight the critical role of representation design in enabling generative models for complex hardware design tasks.

</details>


### [298] [ReasonOps: Operator Segmentation for LLM Reasoning Traces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29192)
*Daniel Lee,Owen Queen,James Zou*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文提出了 ReasonOps，一种无监督提取思维链内部推理结构的方法。研究发现大模型共享 7 种通用的推理操作符，这些操作符构成的序列不仅能揭示模型的“推理指纹”，还能有效预测推理过程的正确性及早期质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的思维链分析方法在描述大规模推理轨迹时，要么过于刻板，要么缺乏足够的表达力，难以捕捉跨模型和跨领域的通用结构特征。因此，研究人员旨在寻找一种能够描述思维链内部结构并提供统一词汇表的方法。

Method: 开发了 ReasonOps 框架，通过对思维链（CoT）中句首 3 token 枢轴点进行无监督聚类，提炼出 7 种通用的推理操作符（如回溯、推断、假设等）。利用该方法分析了 12 个模型的 44,662 条思维链，并结合 LLM 裁判及分类器对这些操作符的分布、预测效能进行验证。

Result: 1. 识别出 7 种跨模型、跨领域的通用推理操作符；2. 发现反射型操作符在难题中表现更好，但在简单问题中反而会降低性能；3. 证明操作符序列具有模型唯一性（即“推理指纹”），可准确识别模型来源；4. 实现基于操作符的准确率预测及早期的质量预估。

Conclusion: ReasonOps 提供了一种无监督的通用推理操作符框架，揭示了大型语言模型在思维链中普遍存在的“推理指纹”，并证明了这些结构化特征在模型识别、性能预测及质量评估方面的显著价值。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought traces from large reasoning models can span tens of thousands of tokens, yet we lack a vocabulary for describing their internal structure. Previous methods developed to analyze chain-of-thought traces are either too rigid or not expressive enough, failing to capture features across domains and models. To remedy this, we develop ReasonOps, an unsupervised, expressive method for annotating chain-of-thought traces, providing succinct universal operators. Using ReasonOps, we analyze 44,662 traces from 12 thinking LLMs spanning 6 families across 8 reasoning benchmarks and discover that they share a common compositional structure: 7 recurring reasoning operators -- discourse-level moves such as backtracking, inferring, and hypothesizing -- that emerge from unsupervised clustering of sentence-initial 3-token pivots. These operators appear across every model family and benchmark domain, confirmed by three independent LLM judges who classify held-out samples at 70 -76% accuracy. We analyze the structure of operators on easy vs. hard problems, revealing that reflective operators are more helpful on hard problems and harm performance on easy problems. Operator sequences are highly model-identifying: a classifier trained on operator distributions alone recovers the source model with macro-AUC, revealing that each model family has a distinctive reasoning fingerprint. Structural operator features predict within-problem answer correctness well above baselines. Classifiers built on these operators reach WP-AUC and on AIME specifically. ReasonOps further enables early quality estimation well before the trace completes: we predict at WP-AUC for only 50% of the trace. The ReasonOps pipeline is unsupervised and annotation-free, enabling deep insights into LLM reasoning traces as well as strong downstream results on model identification and correctness prediction.

</details>


### [299] [DenseSteer: Steering Small Language Models towards Dense Math Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29247)
*Yang Ouyang,Shuhang Lin,Jung-Eun Kim*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文观察到高性能推理模型倾向于采用“稠密推理”模式，并据此提出了DenseSteer框架，通过无需训练的推理时干预，显著提升了小参数模型在数学任务中的推理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大模型展现出强大的思维链（CoT）推理能力，但小参数模型（≤3B）在多步推理任务中表现欠佳。研究旨在探索小模型推理能力提升的内在模式，并寻求一种有效的干预手段以弥补其性能短板。

Method: 提出了一种名为“DenseSteer”的训练无关（training-free）推理时引导框架。该方法通过调节模型内部的表征，使其向“稠密推理”模式对齐，从而在不增加令牌级负对数似然（Negative Log-Likelihood）的前提下，引导小模型生成更高质量、更紧凑的推理路径。

Result: 实验结果表明，DenseSteer 能够有效提升小模型在数学推理基准测试上的准确率，且在保持模型输出似然度不变的情况下，显著优化了推理过程的结构。

Conclusion: “稠密推理”（Dense Reasoning）——即通过减少推理步骤数并提高单步信息密度——是提升小参数模型数学推理能力的一种高效且结构化的方法，无需额外训练即可通过推理时干预实现性能优化。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) demonstrate strong chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning abilities, while smaller models (<= 3B parameters) significantly underperform on multi-step reasoning tasks. Based on empirical analyses of the Qwen-2.5 model family on math reasoning benchmarks, we find that more proficient reasoning is associated with fewer reasoning steps but higher information density per step, a property we term Dense Reasoning. Motivated by this observation, we propose DenseSteer, a training-free inference-time steering framework that enhances small-model reasoning by modulating internal representations toward dense reasoning patterns. Experiments show that our method yields consistent accuracy improvements without increasing token-level Negative Log-Likelihood, highlighting dense reasoning as an effective structural approach to mathematical problem solving.

</details>


### [300] [Differentiable Belief-based Opponent Shaping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29042)
*Aarav G Sane,Karthik Sivachandran,Rohan Paleja*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对多智能体协作中如何影响他人信念的问题，本文提出了 D-BOS 方法。它通过对信念更新过程进行直接求导，让智能体在无需人为定义欺骗目标的情况下，通过环境奖励自动学会如何通过行动影响对手的信念，从而在复杂博弈中实现更优表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的对手塑造方法多集中在对手的参数、策略或值空间，而隐式角色游戏中的信念操纵技术往往依赖硬编码的目标（如欺骗）。研究旨在解决如何在不预设行为意图的前提下，通过战略性行动影响他人的信念，从而实现更高效的多智能体协作。

Method: 提出了一种名为“可微分基于信念的对手塑造”（D-BOS）的方法。该方法将观察者的信念视为被塑造的对手状态，通过对 k 步 Softmax-Bayes 信念动力学进行微分来获得对手塑造信号。此外，通过聚合多个观察者的信念轨迹梯度，该方法能够扩展到多智能体环境，且无需硬编码欺骗或协作目标，而是从环境奖励结构中自然涌现最优策略。

Result: 实验结果表明，在隐式角色游戏中，D-BOS 在性能上超越了基准算法 PPO 和 BBM。特别是在存在冲突利益的混合动机（mixed-motive）环境下，D-BOS 表现出了显著的优势，验证了该方法在塑造对手信念以优化集体或个体回报方面的有效性。

Conclusion: D-BOS 证明了将信念更新过程融入强化学习的梯度优化是可行的，通过直接优化信念状态而非预设行为（如欺骗），能够诱导智能体在多智能体系统中实现更有效的协作与协调。该方法为复杂环境下处理隐式博弈提供了一个通用且有效的框架。

Abstract: Human coordination often relies on the ability to influence the beliefs of others through strategic action. In multi-agent reinforcement learning, opponent shaping attempts to replicate this influence, though existing methods typically operate within an opponent's parameter, policy, or value space. Meanwhile, belief-manipulation techniques in hidden-role games often rely on hard-coded objectives, such as deception or belief saturation. We propose Differentiable Belief-based Opponent Shaping (D-BOS), a first-order method that treats each observer's belief as the shaped opponent state and differentiates through $k$-step softmax-Bayes belief dynamics. Rather than explicitly rewarding deceptive or cooperative behavior, our method treats the belief state as the target for shaping. This allows the optimal strategy to emerge naturally from the environment's reward structure. This belief-space formulation provides an opponent-shaping signal by differentiating through opponent belief updates, and naturally extends to multiple observers by aggregating gradients over their individual inferred belief trajectories. Empirically, D-BOS outperforms PPO and BBM in hidden-role games, with the largest gains in mixed-motive settings.

</details>


### [301] [Better Later Than Sooner: Neuro-Symbolic Knowledge Graph Construction via Ontology-grounded Post-extraction Correction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29168)
*Lorenzo Loconte,Timothy Hospedales,Cristina Cornelio*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于问答系统的神经符号化知识图谱构建框架，通过结合开域抽取、嵌入规范化和针对性的本体论修正，在减少计算成本的同时，解决了传统方法中知识图谱一致性差及难以支持复杂符号化查询的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于文本图的检索增强生成（RAG）方法难以可靠地执行复杂的符号化运算（如聚合或穷举），而现有的基于LLM的知识图谱抽取方法又容易产生违反常识本体论约束的一致性问题。为此，研究者希望开发一种既能保持逻辑一致性，又能降低计算成本的知识图谱构建框架。

Method: 提出了一种神经符号化知识图谱构建框架，包含三个核心阶段：1. 开域信息抽取；2. 基于嵌入的类型与谓词规范化；3. 针对性的基于大模型（LLM）的本体论违规修正。该方法通过将修正步骤置于抽取之后，有效减少了对LLM的重复调用。

Result: 实验结果显示，该方法在保持高质量下游问答能力的同时，显著降低了对LLM的Token消耗，并提高了构建出的知识图谱在SPARQL查询中的适用性。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，通过本体论约束的神经符号化方法构建知识图谱，能显著提高知识图谱的逻辑一致性，并使其更适合执行复杂的SPARQL查询，从而有效地弥补了现有RAG在处理复杂推理和符号化运算时的不足。

Abstract: Question answering (QA) is a core challenge in AI, particularly for complex queries requiring multi-hop reasoning across documents, or symbolic operations like aggregation or exhaustive listing. Retrieval-augmented generation has become the dominant approach to QA, with recent graph-based variants addressing part of these issues by organizing knowledge to better support compositional questions. However, most textual graph-based RAG methods still lack the structure needed for symbolic operations useful to answer complex questions reliably. This motivates symbolic graph-based approaches, which extract knowledge graphs (KGs) whose relations are logic predicates that enable SQL-like querying. Yet these pipelines typically use LLMs for KG extraction, which can introduce consistency issues, where extracted facts may violate commonsense ontology constraints. We propose a neuro-symbolic framework for ontology-grounded KG construction combining open-domain extraction, embedding-based canonicalization of types and predicates, and targeted LLM-based correction of ontology violations. By deferring corrections to a post-extraction stage, our method avoids repeated LLM calls, substantially reducing token usage while improving KG consistency and preserving downstream QA quality. Finally, we show that the extracted KGs are well suited for symbolic querying by measuring the occurrence of SPARQL graph patterns.

</details>


### [302] [PassNet: Scaling Large Language Models for Graph Compiler Pass Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29357)
*Yiqun Liu,Yingsheng Wu,Ruqi Yang,Enrong Zheng,Honglei Qiu,Sijun He,Tai Liang,Jingjing Wu,Yuhan Zhou,Yiwei Zhang,Dongyan Chen,Weihan Yi,Xinqi Li,Siqi Bao*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: PassNet是一个用于生成编译器优化策略的LLM框架。它解决了现有编译器在处理长尾模型时的性能瓶颈，通过大规模数据集和基准测试验证了LLM能够通过图转换优化显著超越传统编译器，且小模型通过微调即可达到顶尖水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代张量编译器（如TorchInductor）在处理主流模型时性能优异，但在面对“长尾”工作负载时表现不佳（43%的子图出现减速）。现有的LLM编译器优化研究多关注单算子生成，而非集成到编译器管线中的图转换优化，缺乏系统性的LLM编译器优化框架。

Method: 1. 提出了PassNet-Dataset：包含来自10万个真实模型中提取的1.8万个独特计算图。
2. 构建了PassBench：包含200个精选的“长尾”可融合任务，并提出了错误感知加速评分（ES_t）作为评估指标。
3. 引入分层完整性防御机制，确保生成的编译器优化策略在正确性和稳定性上满足要求。
4. 利用微调策略，在少量数据轨迹上提升模型性能。

Result: 1. PassBench显示，虽然顶尖LLM在聚合性能上落后于TorchInductor 37%，但在特定子图上可实现高达3倍的加速。
2. 实验证明LLM具备优化潜力，性能受限主要源于生成的一致性。
3. 通过4000条PassNet轨迹对小模型进行微调，实现了2.67倍的性能提升，证明了该方法具有显著的优化空间。

Conclusion: PassNet证明了LLM在编译器优化领域具有巨大的潜力。研究表明，当前LLM在编译器任务上的主要瓶颈在于生成的一致性而非能力不足。通过构建高质量的数据集和评估基准，PassNet为自动化编译器优化提供了关键的基础设施，并验证了利用少量高质量轨迹进行微调即可显著提升模型性能。

Abstract: Modern tensor compilers such as TorchInductor deliver substantial speedups on mainstream models, yet face a systematic performance ceiling on long-tail workloads -- our profiling shows that 43% of real-world subgraphs experience end-to-end slowdowns under default compilation. While LLMs offer a path toward automated optimization, existing efforts focus on standalone kernel generation. We argue that pass generation -- where LLMs author structured graph transformations that integrate directly into compiler pipelines -- is the more appropriate abstraction. We propose PassNet, the first large-scale ecosystem for LLM-based compiler pass generation, comprising: (1) PassNet-Dataset, over 18K unique computational graphs from 100K real-world models; and (2) PassBench, 200 curated long-tail fusible tasks (comprising 2,060 subgraphs in total) evaluated under the Error-aware Speedup Score (ES_t) -- a metric unifying correctness, stability, and performance -- with layered integrity defenses against systematic LLM exploitation. Experiments reveal that PassBench is both highly discriminative and genuinely unsaturated: the best frontier model trails TorchInductor by 37% in aggregate, yet on individual subgraphs LLMs achieve up to 3x speedup over the same compiler -- indicating that the bottleneck is consistency, not capability. Fine-tuning a small model on merely ~4K PassNet trajectories yields a 2.67x improvement approaching frontier-model performance, demonstrating substantial headroom and validating PassNet as live training infrastructure for advancing LLM-driven compiler optimization. All data, benchmarks, and tooling are publicly available.

</details>

### [303] [CrossAlpha: An Annual-Report Benchmark for Cross-Market Factor Research](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29286)
*Qian Wang,Zhongyi Tong,Nuo Chen,Zhaomin Wu,Bingsheng He*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出了CrossAlpha，这是一个针对跨市场因子研究的首个标准化基准测试，通过对异构财报进行语义蒸馏、构建去偏见的跨市场企业关系图，并严格进行跨时区交易对齐，有效证明了利用跨市场披露信息可以显著提升股票回报预测的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有金融研究缺乏支持“披露信息到回报预测”的跨市场基准。跨市场研究面临诸多挑战：不同市场间文件语言和监管差异巨大、披露内容存在行业共性偏见，以及必须解决跨市场间的实际交易时间对齐问题。因此，作者旨在构建一个标准化的跨市场金融因子研究基准。

Method: 该论文提出了CrossAlpha基准测试，包含三个核心组件：1. 披露蒸馏（Disclosure Distillation）：利用大模型将不同语言和监管体系下的异构年度报告标准化为十类英语业务描述；2. 残差模式图构建（Residual Schema Graph Construction）：通过主成分分析（PCA）白化处理，构建消除通用披露偏见的跨市场企业对相似度分数；3. 时间对齐评估（Timing-Aligned Evaluation）：结合11年的日线OHLCV数据，建立符合实际跨市场交易时序的可行性验证机制。

Result: 在US-to-Japan（美国到日本）的实验设置中，基于CrossAlpha提取的跨市场同行信号表现优异（ICIR达到0.39），显著超过了基于国内文本、行业代码及回报相关性的传统基准（0.07-0.18）。此外，在大多数目标市场中，跨市场来源的预测能力均超过了单一市场内的文本基准。该数据集涵盖了美、日、台、韩、港五个市场的约3600家企业。

Conclusion: CrossAlpha 是一个开源且可复用的基准测试，填补了跨市场金融NLP研究的空白，证明了从跨市场披露信息中提取的信号具有超越传统国内同类指标（如行业代码或价格相关性）的预测能力，为跨市场因子研究提供了标准化的评估框架。

Abstract: Cross-market factor research studies whether firm-level signals from one or more markets can predict returns in a target market, but existing public benchmarks do not support cross-market disclosure-to-return evaluation. Building such a benchmark is challenging because filings differ across languages and regulatory systems, disclosure-derived similarity can be biased by common reporting components, and cross-market signals must be evaluated under feasible trading-time alignment. We introduce \textbf{CrossAlpha}, a public annual-report benchmark for cross-market factor research. CrossAlpha addresses these challenges through three corresponding components: \emph{Disclosure Distillation}, which standardises heterogeneous filings into ten-category English business descriptions; \emph{Residual Schema Graph Construction}, which builds PCA-whitened cross-market firm-pair scores from schema-level disclosures; and \emph{Timing-Aligned Evaluation}, which pairs the graph with 11 years of daily OHLCV data to construct forward-return labels under feasible cross-market execution protocols. CrossAlpha covers about 3,600 firms and 10,700 firm-year reports from the United States, Japan, Taiwan, South Korea, and Hong Kong, and releases about 19M directed firm-pair scores. In experiments, disclosure-derived cross-market peers outperform domestic text, industry-code, and return-correlation peers in the US-to-Japan setting (ICIR 0.39 versus 0.07--0.18), and cross-market sources beat the domestic text baseline in most target markets. CrossAlpha offers an open-sourced, reusable, return-grounded benchmark for cross-market financial NLP.

</details>


### [304] [FLASH-MAXSIM: IO-Aware Fused Kernels for Late-Interaction Scoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29517)
*Roi Pony,Adi Raz Goldfarb,Idan Friedman,Daniel Ezer,Udi Barzelay*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: Flash-MaxSim 通过融合 GPU 内核消除了延迟交互检索中昂贵的相似度张量内存开销，实现了显著的性能加速与显存节省，且完全保留了检索精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的延迟交互检索模型（如 ColBERT、ColPali）在计算时需在 GPU 内存中物化巨大的查询-文档相似度张量，导致极高的显存占用，严重限制了批处理规模和推理/训练效率。

Method: 提出了一种 IO 感知且融合的 GPU 内核 Flash-MaxSim，通过在片上 SRAM 中以分块（tiling）方式流式处理查询与文档向量，消除了显存中对完整相似度张量的物化需求；并在反向传播中采用基于反向网格 CSR 构造的梯度规约方法，同时支持 INT8 量化和变长处理。

Result: Flash-MaxSim 在 A100 和 H100 GPU 上分别实现了高达 3.9 倍和 4.7 倍的加速，推理显存使用降低至 1/16，训练显存降低至约 1/28，并保持了与 FP32 基准 100% 的 Top-20 排序一致性。

Conclusion: Flash-MaxSim 是一种高效的 GPU 计算范式，通过内存优化和内核融合彻底解决了延迟交互检索（如 ColBERT 和 ColPali）中的内存瓶颈问题，在保持检索精度的同时大幅提升了吞吐量并降低了内存开销。

Abstract: Late-interaction retrieval (ColBERT, ColPali) scores a query against a document with the MaxSim operator: for every query token, the maximum similarity over the document tokens, summed over
  query tokens. The standard implementation materializes the full query-token x document-token similarity tensor in GPU memory; for visual ColPali at 10K documents this tensor alone is 21 GB in
  FP16, created only to be reduced to one score per document and discarded. It exhausts a 40 GB GPU and bounds the achievable batch size in both inference and training. We present
  Flash-MaxSim, an IO-aware fused GPU kernel that computes exactly the same scores without ever materializing the tensor, by streaming query and document tiles through on-chip SRAM and folding
  the row-maximum reduction into the same pass. We extend the IO-aware principle through the training backward pass, an inverse-grid CSR construction that reuses the forward argmax for an
  atomic-free, destination-owned gradient reduction, and through INT8xINT8 quantization and variable-length (padding-free) scoring. Flash-MaxSim is up to 3.9x faster on an A100 (4.7x on an
  H100) than naive PyTorch at matched precision, uses up to 16x less inference memory and ~28x less training memory, unlocks corpus and batch sizes that exhaust PyTorch entirely, preserves the
  exact ranking (100% top-20 agreement with an FP32 reference)

</details>


### [305] [No More K-means:Single-Stage Sparse Coding for Efficient Multi-Vector Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30120)
*Lixuan Guo,Yifei Wang,Tiansheng Wen,Aosong Feng,Stefanie Jegelka,Chenyu You*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种名为SSR的单阶段稀疏检索方法，通过使用稀疏自动编码器（SAE）取代传统的聚类和降维技术，在大幅缩减索引时间和检索延迟的同时，提升了大规模语料库的信息检索精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对当前多向量检索（MVR）模型（如ColBERT）在处理大规模语料时面临的存储成本高、聚类耗时长以及降维带来的语义损失等问题，旨在寻求一种无需聚类且能保持检索精度的替代方案。

Method: 提出单阶段稀疏检索（SSR）方法，利用稀疏自动编码器（SAE）将token嵌入映射为高维稀疏表示，从而完全摒弃了传统的向量聚类（如K-means）和降维操作，并结合倒排索引实现高效的检索流程。

Result: 在BEIR基准测试中，SSR相较于ColBERTv2实现了15倍的索引速度提升，检索延迟降低了一半，同时在检索性能指标上优于主流基线模型，实现了性能与效率的协同优化。

Conclusion: SSR通过引入稀疏自动编码器（SAE）实现了多向量检索范式的升级，通过将高维稀疏特征与倒排索引结合，成功解决了传统方法在存储效率、索引速度与检索精度之间的权衡难题，为大规模信息检索提供了更高效、更精准的解决方案。

Abstract: Multi-vector retrieval (MVR) models, exemplified by ColBERT, have established new benchmarks in retrieval accuracy by preserving fine-grained token-level interactions. However, this granularity imposes prohibitive storage and retrieval efficiency bottlenecks: to manage the immense memory footprint and computational overhead of billion-scale token vectors, state-of-the-art systems are forced to rely on aggressive dimension reduction and complex clustering (e.g., K-means). This compromise introduces two critical limitations: excessive indexing latency of clustering large-scale corpora and semantic information loss inherent to compression. In this paper, we propose Single-stage Sparse Retrieval (SSR}, a paradigm shift that replaces expensive clustering with efficient sparse coding. Instead of compressing features into low-dimensional dense vectors, we utilize Sparse Autoencoder (SAE) to project token embeddings into a high-dimensional but highly sparse representation. This transformation enables us to bypass vector clustering entirely and leverage inverted indexing for precise, high-throughput retrieval. Extensive experiments on the BEIR benchmark demonstrate that SSR achieves a "trifecta" of improvements: it reduces indexing time by 15x compared to ColBERTv2, halves retrieval latency, and simultaneously improves retrieval performance over leading baselines.

</details>


### [306] [Latent Terms: Dense Retrievers Contain Trivially Extractable BM25-ready Zipfian Vocabularies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29384)
*Benjamin Clavié,Sean Lee,Aamir Shakir,Makoto P. Kato*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 研究人员提出了一种名为“潜在术语”（Latent Terms）的方法，通过在密集检索模型上使用稀疏自编码器，无需额外训练即可将模型表示转换为高效的稀疏检索特征，在提升检索性能的同时实现了更好的模型可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有密集检索模型虽然性能强大，但其内部表示的结构往往是“黑盒”，且难以直接利用传统的高效稀疏索引技术。研究人员旨在探究密集检索模型中是否隐含着可直接用于稀疏检索的结构化信息，并试图通过无需额外监督学习的方法将其提取出来。

Method: 提出了“潜在术语”（Latent Terms）方法。该方法不对检索器进行特定调整，而是直接在预训练好的密集检索模型上应用稀疏自编码器（Sparse Autoencoders），将密集表示分解为可用于BM25等经典稀疏检索评分的“潜在词汇表”（Latent Vocabulary），且无需额外的稀疏检索监督或特定的扩展目标。

Result: 实验结果表明，Latent Terms 方法提取的潜在词汇表现出近似 Zipf 定律的统计特性。在检索性能上，该方法不仅能匹配或超越基础模型原有的密集评分，在处理单向量检索失效场景（如 LIMIT 任务）时也显著优于基础模型，并能与主流的稀疏检索模型（如 SPLADE）相媲美。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了密集检索模型内部蕴含着比默认评分函数所展现的更为丰富的结构，通过稀疏自编码器可以有效地提取这些可解释的稀疏特征，从而弥合了密集与稀疏检索之间的范式鸿沟，为模型的可解释性和检索性能优化提供了新思路。

Abstract: We propose Latent Terms, a method revealing that models trained for dense retrieval, whether single- or multi-vector, learn representations that can trivially be decomposed into retrieval-ready sparse features. When trained on frozen retrievers, Sparse Autoencoders without any retrieval-specific adjustments extract a latent vocabulary with approximately Zipfian collection statistics, directly suitable for classical sparse retrieval scoring via BM25. This approach enables sparse retrieval while requiring no learned expansion objective or sparse retrieval supervision whatsoever, and can be readily applied to any dense retriever. Latent Terms is able to match or outperform single-vector scoring methods from its own base model as well as comparable SPLADE variants. In addition, it substantially outperforms its base model on LIMIT, a task specifically designed to highlight the failures of single-vector retrieval. Overall, our results highlight that neural retrievers contain more expressive and indexable structure than their default scoring functions expose, but that other methods can nonetheless be leveraged.

</details>


### [307] [GRASP: Plan-Guided Graph Retrieval with Adaptive Fusion and Reranking on Semi-Structured Knowledge Bases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30237)
*Yicheng Tao,Yiqun Wang,Xiangchen Song,Xin Luo,Kai Liu,Jie Liu*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 GRASP 的三阶段 SKB 检索框架，通过协同利用图检索、条件融合和重排序，显著提升了半结构化知识库的检索性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的半结构化知识库（SKB）混合检索系统往往孤立地使用图信息或文本信息，缺乏有效的深度集成机制，导致检索性能受限，无法充分发挥图结构与文本语义互补的优势。

Method: 本文提出了 GRASP 框架，包含三个阶段：1. 基于计划的图检索（Plan-based Graph Retrieval）；2. 计划条件下的融合检索（Plan-conditioned Fusion with Dense Retriever）；3. 对融合候选结果进行精细化的重排序（Fine-tuned Reranker）。

Result: GRASP 在 STaRK 基准测试的所有指标上均显著超越了现有最先进技术（SOTA），其中平均 Hit@1 从 62.0 提升至 73.9，且通过消融实验验证了该框架的有效性和鲁棒性。

Conclusion: GRASP 通过将图检索、条件融合和重排序三个阶段有机结合，证明了在半结构化知识库（SKB）中协同利用图结构信息和文本语义检索的优越性，为构建更高效的混合检索系统提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Semi-structured knowledge bases (SKBs) embed textual documents in a typed graph of entities and relations, and underpin applications such as product search, academic paper search, and precision-medicine inquiries. Existing hybrid retrieval systems on SKBs either use the graph only for query expansion, mix textual and structural branches under a global weighting, or rely on fine-tuned graph-traversal generators. We present GRASP, a three-stage SKB retrieval framework unifying plan-based graph retrieval, plan-conditioned fusion with a dense retriever, and a fine-tuned reranker over the fused candidates. GRASP substantially advances the state of the art on every metric across the three STaRK benchmarks, lifting average Hit@1 from 62.0 to 73.9. Ablation and sensitivity studies further confirm the effectiveness and robustness of GRASP.

</details>


### [308] [Generative Spatiotemporal Intent Sequence Recommendation via Implicit Reasoning in Amap](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28888)
*Sicong Wang,Ruiting Dong,Yue Liu,Bowen Zheng,Jun Meng,Jie Li,Shuaijun Guo,Yu Gu,Fanyi Di,Xin Li*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出了 GPlan 框架，通过隐式思维链蒸馏和反事实偏好优化，使轻量级模型具备了大型语言模型的复杂时空推理能力，解决了实时意图推荐中的延迟高与物理不可行问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在实际应用中，用户行为具有复杂的时空依赖性，即意图流。利用大模型进行此类推荐存在推理延迟高、计划缺乏物理可行性及上下文不匹配等问题，难以满足工业场景的实时需求。

Method: 提出了 GPlan 框架，包含两个核心模块：1. 渐进式隐式思维链蒸馏（Progressive Implicit CoT Distillation）：将大模型的复杂推理过程压缩进潜空间表征中，无需生成冗长的文本即可实现逻辑传承；2. 时空反事实偏好优化（Spatiotemporal Counterfactual DPO）：通过反事实情境与计划对，引导模型学习时空约束，增强模型对环境的敏感度。

Result: 线下实验与线上 A/B 测试表明，GPlan 能够生成更具连贯性的意图序列，显著降低了与时空上下文冲突的计划比例，有效平衡了模型性能与推理速度。

Conclusion: GPlan 通过蒸馏与强化学习对齐策略，成功将大型语言模型的推理能力迁移至轻量级模型，在保持低延迟的同时，显著提升了时空意图序列推荐的逻辑连贯性与现实可行性，为工业界部署复杂序列生成任务提供了有效的范式。

Abstract: Real-world user behavior rarely consists of isolated actions; instead, it often forms intent flows governed by spatiotemporal dependencies. To provide integrated service recommendations, we focus on the task of Generative Spatiotemporal Intent Sequence Recommendation (GSISR), which aims to generate intent sequences that are logically coherent and physically executable within complex spatiotemporal contexts. While LLMs offer strong reasoning potential for GSISR, direct industrial deployment is limited by high inference latency and context-mismatched or physically infeasible plans. To address these challenges, we propose a generative framework, GPlan, that internalizes LLM reasoning into lightweight models through two components. First, to enable reasoning under strict latency constraints, we introduce Progressive Implicit CoT Distillation, which compresses explicit reasoning processes into reserved latent tokens, allowing small models to inherit complex planning logic without generating long reasoning text. Second, to address the disconnect between general knowledge and real-world constraints, we design Spatiotemporal Counterfactual DPO. By aligning the model with counterfactual context-plan pairs, we improve sensitivity to spatiotemporal context and reduce context-mismatched plans. Offline experiments and online A/B testing demonstrate that our approach improves sequence coherence and context responsiveness. Our implementation and the anonymized GSISR dataset are available at https://github.com/alibaba/GPlan.

</details>


### [309] [Toward User Preference Alignment in LLM Recommendation via Explicit Context Feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29141)
*Weizhi Zhang,Wooseong Yang,Yuxin Cui,Zhaohui Guo,Hins Hu,Liangwei Yang,Henry Peng Zou,Qifei Wang,Hanqing Zeng,Jiayi Liu,Yinglong Xia,Philip S. Yu*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文旨在推动下一代推荐系统转型，主张通过大语言模型充分挖掘并利用用户评论等显式上下文反馈，以解决传统推荐系统对用户偏好理解不足及信息茧房问题，实现更透明、可解释的个性化推荐。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统推荐系统主要依赖隐式信号，忽略了用户通过文本提供的显式上下文反馈。这种忽视导致系统难以理解用户偏好的深层语义，造成偏好错位并加剧“过滤泡沫”现象。尽管大语言模型（LLM）发展迅速，但现有方法仍过度依赖元数据而未充分挖掘用户生成的丰富文本信息。

Method: 本文采取了综述与框架设计相结合的方法：回顾了推荐系统的演变历程，分析了显式上下文反馈的价值，呼吁建立新的评估基准与指标，并提出了一套将显式用户信号整合到可扩展的大模型驱动推荐系统中的框架。

Result: 本文确立了以显式上下文反馈为核心的下一代大模型推荐系统范式，明确了其在提升推荐准确性、多样性及可解释性方面的巨大潜力，并为构建更具人性化与透明度的在线平台指明了技术发展方向。

Conclusion: 文章强调，未来的推荐系统应从单纯依赖隐式行为数据转向充分利用显式上下文反馈（如用户评论）。通过整合大语言模型（LLM）的语义理解能力，能够构建出更个性化、透明且具备可解释性的下一代推荐系统，从而有效解决过滤泡沫问题。

Abstract: Traditional recommender systems (RecSys) primarily infer user preferences from implicit signals (such as clicks, watches, and purchases), often neglecting the rich explicit contextual feedback users provide through verbal text, like comments and reviews. This explicit context feedback captures the nuanced reasons behind user decisions regarding their preferences. In addition, it offers critical heterogeneous information for user preference alignment and more explainable recommendations. Overlooking such signals can lead to misaligned user preferences and further reinforce filter bubbles, as algorithms fail to understand the "semantic context" behind user choices. Recent advances in Large Language Models (LLMs) present new opportunities to harness user-generated content for more accurate and diverse recommendations, yet current LLM-based recommendations still focus on using item meta-data and underutilize this resource. In this paper, we advocate for prioritizing explicit context feedback in the next generation of LLM-based RecSys. We review the evolution of recommendation paradigms, highlight the value of context-rich feedback, call for new benchmarks and metrics, and introduce frameworks for integrating explicit user signals into scalable LLM-driven RecSys. Centering on user-preference modeling, we aim to foster more personalized, transparent, and explainable RecSys online platforms.

</details>
